    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2661371820" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2661371820" />
    <a title="☆ Todd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12415682-todd"><img alt="☆ Todd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539502816p2/12415682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2661371820?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Todd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Todd" href="/user/show/12415682-todd">☆ Todd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12415682-todd?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2661371820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1522740966783299915"><br/><b>Wow, this book was <i>EVEN BETTER</i> than I had dared hope. : )</b><br/><br/><a href='https://imgur.com/VN0vY3q' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552895846ra/27222402.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'd initially held off on requesting this book until early reviews hit Goodreads because: <br/><br/><b>1.) Royal*anything* usually bores me to tears.<br/><br/>2.) So do books involving politics of any shape or form.</b><br/><br/>But this story was a delicious mix of <b>drama, angst, excitement</b> and, most importantly, <b>hope</b>.<br/><br/>I loved both <b>First Son Alex</b> and <b>HRH Prince Henry</b> right from the get go, as they first <b>snarked</b> their way into my heart, then as feelings began to develop, ga</span>
  <span id="freeText1522740966783299915" style="display:none"><br><b>Wow, this book was <i>EVEN BETTER</i> than I had dared hope. : )</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/VN0vY3q" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552895846ra/27222402.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'd initially held off on requesting this book until early reviews hit Goodreads because: <br><br><b>1.) Royal*anything* usually bores me to tears.<br><br>2.) So do books involving politics of any shape or form.</b><br><br>But this story was a delicious mix of <b>drama, angst, excitement</b> and, most importantly, <b>hope</b>.<br><br>I loved both <b>First Son Alex</b> and <b>HRH Prince Henry</b> right from the get go, as they first <b>snarked</b> their way into my heart, then as feelings began to develop, gave me enough <b>banter</b> to keep me laughing every few pages.<br><br>[Mexican-American Alex:]<br><a href="https://imgur.com/81UWXqh" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552895982i/27222407._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I also found the <b>side characters</b> to be a delight, from First Daughter June to Second Daughter Nora to Princess Beatrice to Alex's parents and friends. They were all worthy of their places in the story, only adding to my level of interest.<br><br>As the story began, Alex's intense dislike for <i>"<b>HRH Prince Dickhead</b>"</i> wasn't really addressed in-depth; however, once their first meeting was detailed out, I have to admit that I didn't care much for Henry, either.<br><br>Then after they were <b>forced to spend time together</b> as pretend BFF's, trying to undo damage to international relations at a Royal wedding, Henry's staunch façade began to slip and we got to see glimpses of the boy behind the unfeeling, arrogant mask. And I *loved* him from there on out.<br><br>[Prince Henry:]<br><a href="https://imgur.com/JdbavZr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552896165i/27222434._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was basically your <b>"<i>boy is enamored of boy, finally meets boy, get slighted by boy, hates boy, then they work through their shit, eventually falling madly in love</i>"</b> story and it totally worked for me.<br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/4COud3p" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552896576i/27222470.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yes, there was lots of political speak, with Alex's mother being POTUS, and Henry's grandmother being the Queen of England, but it never got to be too much, as <b>humor, feelings, and just... *realness* permeated the pages</b>.<br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/08Fjn7P" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552896165ra/27222435.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There was also <b>a ton of political intrigue, with an unexpected act of betrayal</b>, which I felt made the book more than less interesting for me. That was a big ole' shock and a departure from my norm, let me tell you.<br><br>For all of you <b>Steam Queens</b> out there, while the sex scenes were not entirely fade to black, they were definitely <b>more *emotive* than descriptive or explicit</b>. If I'm remembering correctly, I don't think the book even contained the words 'penis' or 'dick', other than when Alex would adoringly call Henry a dickhead. I was actually fine with the lack of traditional heat, though.<br><br>I did have a few niggles, Firstly, at 432 (reported) pages, <b>the story felt suuuuuper long</b>, although I never found myself bored. At times, the pacing felt a bit on the slow side, but the humor did its job in keeping me engaged.<br><br>Secondly, <b>PRESENT TENSE</b>. Ugh. ‘Nuff said.<br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/WPB3utX" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552896165ra/27222436.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lastly, OMMFG, Henry's propensity to imitate Carl Lewis, <b>pulling a runner and ghosting Alex</b> on more than one occasion, nearly <b>drove me to goddamn drink</b>. True story.<br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/a10HtyE" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552896794i/27222484.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But Alex wasn't one to be ignored, fortunately, so<b> if a bitch needed read, he was the right man for the job</b>, always pulling these two adorable dumbasses back onto The Road to True Love, capitalized, because it's '<i>a thing</i>' .<br><br>I'm extremely happy that I stepped out of my usual comfort zone and gave this book a chance, and would rate it at around <b>4.75 stars for the humor and feels</b>.<br><br>-----------------------------------------------<br><br><i>My ARC copy of the book was provided by the publisher in exchange for a fair, unbiased review.</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/12415682-todd?order=d&amp;sort=date_read&amp;view=reviews" rel="nofollow noopener">See All My Latest Reads (Review Quick-Links)</a><br><br>-----------------------------------------------</span>
  <a data-text-id="1522740966783299915" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('R8S1amY6UzUQhYUeb9clDSF5K9xTPHK7i+yKN9f4YESWloYcVnPyzT8SrMzTOjrDbjVghip3JUX1NaRxzKnDUQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oi0cLzNgi4dnB2/uAbrbiEnn4uz0yhKiw4wh7lPAJDpzfy9ZAykqf0iQRjy9V8RGBqupto2BRVy9VQ+oSJGHLw==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer7960731213223453912">Casey McQuiston is a New York Times bestselling author of romantic comedies and a pie entusiast. She writes stories about smart people with bad manners falling in love. Born and raised in southern Louisiana, she now lives in New York City with her poodle mix/personal assistant, Pepper.</span>
